2025-02-17T03:16:44.8541442Z [1;31mSwitching to the Multi-user Installer[0m
2025-02-17T03:16:44.8643420Z [32mWelcome to the Multi-User Nix Installation
2025-02-17T03:16:44.8654546Z [0m
2025-02-17T03:16:44.8655053Z This installation tool will set up your computer with the Nix package
2025-02-17T03:16:44.8655696Z manager. This will happen in a few stages:
2025-02-17T03:16:44.8656022Z 
2025-02-17T03:16:44.8656295Z 1. Make sure your computer doesn't already have Nix. If it does, I
2025-02-17T03:16:44.8657014Z    will show you instructions on how to clean up your old install.
2025-02-17T03:16:44.8657433Z 
2025-02-17T03:16:44.8657702Z 2. Show you what I am going to install and where. Then I will ask
2025-02-17T03:16:44.8658255Z    if you are ready to continue.
2025-02-17T03:16:44.8658529Z 
2025-02-17T03:16:44.8659052Z 3. Create the system users [34m(uids [30001..30004])[0m and groups [34m(gid 30000)[0m
2025-02-17T03:16:44.8659973Z    that the Nix daemon uses to run builds.
2025-02-17T03:16:44.8660487Z 
2025-02-17T03:16:44.8660637Z 4. Perform the basic installation of the Nix files daemon.
2025-02-17T03:16:44.8661013Z 
2025-02-17T03:16:44.8661186Z 5. Configure your shell to import special Nix Profile files, so you
2025-02-17T03:16:44.8661527Z    can use Nix.
2025-02-17T03:16:44.8661637Z 
2025-02-17T03:16:44.8661725Z 6. Start the Nix daemon.
2025-02-17T03:16:44.8661861Z 
2025-02-17T03:16:44.8662120Z [32m[4;32mWould you like to see a more detailed list of what I will do?
2025-02-17T03:16:44.8662512Z [0mNo TTY, assuming you would say yes :)
2025-02-17T03:16:44.8667824Z 
2025-02-17T03:16:44.8668123Z I will:
2025-02-17T03:16:44.8668326Z 
2025-02-17T03:16:44.8668574Z  - make sure your computer doesn't already have Nix files
2025-02-17T03:16:44.8669186Z    (if it does, I will tell you how to clean them up.)
2025-02-17T03:16:44.8669985Z  - create local users (see the list above for the users I'll make)
2025-02-17T03:16:44.8670540Z  - create a local group (nixbld)
2025-02-17T03:16:44.8670812Z  - install Nix in to /nix
2025-02-17T03:16:44.8671078Z  - create a configuration file in /etc/nix
2025-02-17T03:16:44.8671439Z  - set up the "default profile" by creating some Nix-related files in
2025-02-17T03:16:44.8671766Z    /root
2025-02-17T03:16:44.8685857Z  - back up /etc/bash.bashrc to /etc/bash.bashrc.backup-before-nix
2025-02-17T03:16:44.8686320Z  - update /etc/bash.bashrc to include some Nix configuration
2025-02-17T03:16:44.8697408Z  - load and start a service (at /etc/systemd/system/nix-daemon.service
2025-02-17T03:16:44.8697874Z    and /etc/systemd/system/nix-daemon.socket) for nix-daemon
2025-02-17T03:16:44.8698111Z 
2025-02-17T03:16:44.8700109Z [32m[4;32mReady to continue?
2025-02-17T03:16:44.8700649Z [0mNo TTY, assuming you would say yes :)
